   589→AI: [2026-03-04 10:40:52]
   590→核心结论先给你
   591→Gitea 对服务器的硬件要求极低，是同类自托管 Git / 协作平台中资源占用最小的工业级产品之一—— 最低仅需 256MB 内存就能启动运行，甚至可以在树莓派这类低功耗嵌入式设备上流畅使用；哪怕是面向中小团队的生产环境，基础配置就能完全 hold 住，完全适配你做「企业私有部署、非技术用户协作平台」的核心需求
   592→。
   593→一、分场景的服务器配置要求
   594→1. 最低可运行配置（测试 / 个人极简场景）
   595→仅用于个人测试、单人使用，不涉及高并发、大量 CI/CD 任务：
   596→CPU：1 核（x86/arm/arm64 均可，树莓派 3/4/5 都能跑）
   597→内存：256MB 可启动，512MB 即可稳定运行
   598→存储：10GB 以上存储空间（机械硬盘也能跑，SSD 优先）
   599→系统：Linux/macOS/Windows/FreeBSD 全平台兼容
   600→2. 官方推荐生产环境配置（按团队规模划分）
   601→结合 Gitea 官方文档与国内生产环境实践，匹配你做企业私有部署的场景，配置如下
   602→：
   603→表格
   604→团队 / 用户规模	推荐 CPU 核心	推荐内存	推荐存储	配套数据库	适用场景
   605→1-10 人（个人 / 小团队）	2 核	2-4GB	50-100GB SSD	SQLite/MySQL	一人公司、小部门、小项目，日常任务 / 文档 / 协作使用
   606→10-50 人（中小团队）	2-4 核	4-8GB	100-200GB SSD	MySQL/PostgreSQL	中小型企业全公司部署，多项目、多部门协作，轻度 CI/CD 使用
   607→50-200 人（中大型团队）	4-8 核	8-16GB	500GB-1TB SSD	PostgreSQL + Redis 缓存	中大型企业，高频并发操作，大量仓库 / 附件，常规 CI/CD 任务
   608→200 人以上（大型企业）	8 核以上	16-32GB	2TB 以上 SSD	集群化 PostgreSQL + Redis + 对象存储	多分支机构、高并发、大规模 CI/CD 流水线，高可用集群部署
   609→3. 真实生产环境的资源占用参考
   610→Gitea 的实际资源占用远低于同类产品，空跑和常规使用的负载极低：
   611→空服务启动后：内存占用仅 100-300MB，CPU 占用几乎可以忽略，启动时间 10 秒内
   612→10 人以内小团队常规使用：内存占用稳定在 300-800MB，CPU 占用长期低于 20%
   613→搭配 PostgreSQL 数据库：数据库额外占用仅 100-200MB，整套服务 1 核 2GB 的服务器就能流畅跑满全功能
   614→二、影响 Gitea 资源占用的核心因素（避坑重点）
   615→Gitea 的基础服务本身极度省资源，真正会拉高服务器负载的，是你开启的附加功能和使用场景，结合你的产品规划，重点关注这几点：
   616→Gitea Actions（CI/CD 流水线）这是资源占用的第一大头。如果你的平台要给用户提供自动化任务、AI 生成代码、自动归档等能力，大量跑工作流会显著消耗 CPU 和内存。
   617→优化方案：把 Actions Runner 单独部署，不要和 Gitea 主服务共用一台服务器，主服务只做调度，不执行任务，彻底避免 CI 任务抢占主服务资源。
   618→并发用户数与高频操作日常浏览、发帖、看任务、查看文档，对资源消耗极低；但大量用户同时提交内容、上传大文件、对比版本差异，会临时拉高 CPU 和 IO 负载。
   619→优化方案：用 SSD 硬盘提升随机读写性能，开启 Gzip 压缩，配置 Redis 缓存热点数据，大幅降低数据库和磁盘 IO 压力。
   620→Git LFS 大文件存储纯文本（Markdown 文档、任务内容、对话记录）对存储的消耗极小，Git 本身有高效的压缩机制，哪怕几万条文档也占不了多少空间；但如果用户大量上传视频、PPT、设计稿、安装包等大文件，会快速占用存储和带宽。
   621→优化方案：开启 Git LFS，把大文件存储到独立的对象存储（如 MinIO、阿里云 OSS），不占用主服务器的存储和 IO 资源。
   622→仓库数量与小文件占用Git 天生会生成大量小文件，哪怕单个文件只有几 KB，也会占用一个磁盘 inode，一旦 inode 耗尽，哪怕磁盘还有空间，服务也会崩溃。
   623→优化方案：
   624→数据目录单独挂载一块磁盘，不要放在系统根分区；
   625→定期执行 Git 仓库垃圾回收（git gc），清理无用的松散对象；
   626→限制单用户 / 单项目的仓库创建数量，避免指数级增长。
   627→数据库选型
   628→10 人以内小团队：用内置的 SQLite 即可，无需额外部署数据库，最省资源；
   629→10 人以上团队：必须用 MySQL/PostgreSQL，性能更稳定，并发支持更好，避免 SQLite 的锁表问题。
   630→三、和同类产品的资源占用对比（直观参考）
   631→结合你的需求，和主流的协作 / 开发平台做对比，Gitea 的轻量优势极其明显：
   632→表格
   633→产品	最低生产配置	空服务内存占用	部署复杂度	适配你的需求的匹配度
   634→Gitea	1 核 512MB 内存	100-300MB	极低，单二进制 / 单 Docker 容器一键启动	极高，完全可控、可定制、轻量，私有部署成本极低
   635→GitLab CE	4 核 8GB 内存	4GB 起步	极高，多容器编排，依赖组件多	极低，资源占用高，定制化难，完全面向技术人员
   636→Spring 若依等后台框架	2 核 4GB 内存	500MB+（仅框架本身）	中等，需要从零开发所有业务功能	中等，仅提供基础骨架，核心协作能力要自己开发，最终资源占用取决于你的开发质量
   637→飞书 / Notion	无私有部署选项（仅超大企业可定制，成本极高）	无	无，纯 SaaS 服务	极低，数据不可控，完全无法定制化
   638→四、结合你的产品规划的部署优化建议
   639→针对你要做的「OpenClaw 做 AI 大脑 + Gitea 做资产底座 + 非技术用户友好的协作平台」，给你 3 个最贴合的落地建议，兼顾性能、成本和稳定性：
   640→最小化起步方案（MVP 验证阶段）直接用 2 核 4GB 内存、50GB SSD 的云服务器 / 本地服务器，就能跑通完整功能：
   641→主服务：Gitea + PostgreSQL 数据库，占用不超过 1GB 内存；
   642→AI 中枢：OpenClaw 服务，占用 1-2GB 内存；
   643→剩余资源留作并发缓冲和轻度 Actions 任务，完全足够 10-20 人的小团队测试使用，月服务器成本极低。
   644→生产环境拆分部署（正式商用阶段）把核心服务和高负载服务分开，避免互相影响，同时控制成本：
   645→主服务器：2 核 4GB，只跑 Gitea 主服务和数据库，处理用户请求、权限管理、仓库存储，保证核心服务稳定不卡顿；
   646→任务服务器：单独一台服务器跑 OpenClaw 和 Gitea Actions Runner，处理 AI 生成、自动化任务、工作流执行，哪怕任务跑崩了，也不会影响主服务；
   647→存储：大文件 / 附件用独立的对象存储，主服务器只存文本数据，进一步降低负载。
   648→功能裁剪，进一步降低资源占用针对非技术用户，关闭 Gitea 里用不到的技术向功能，不仅能简化前端体验，还能减少资源消耗：
   649→关闭不需要的功能：如容器镜像仓库、代码扫描、SSH 密钥管理（普通用户用不到）；
   650→限制并发和资源：通过 Docker 或 systemd 限制 Gitea 的 CPU / 内存上限，避免异常操作占满服务器资源；
   651→优化 Go 运行参数：调整 GOGC 和 GOMEMLIMIT 参数，在低内存环境下也能稳定运行。
   652→最后总结
   653→Gitea 对服务器的要求，完全可以用「丰俭由人」来形容：
   654→个人测试、小团队使用，最低配的服务器甚至树莓派就能跑，几乎零成本；
   655→中小企业生产使用，常规的 2 核 4GB 服务器就能完全 hold 住，部署和维护成本极低；
   656→哪怕是千人级的大型企业，也只需要常规的企业级服务器就能支撑，远低于 GitLab 等同类产品的硬件要求。
   657→完全匹配你做「企业私有部署、非技术用户协作、数字资产沉淀」的核心需求，不会因为硬件门槛限制你的产品落地。
   658→需要我给你一份适配 2 核 4GB 服务器的 Docker Compose 一键部署脚本（含 PostgreSQL、资源限制、基础安全配置），你直接复制就能用吗？

## 1. GITEA-RELATED IDEAS (Major Focus)

### Core Vision: Gitea as Universal Office Collaboration Platform

The most significant concept emerging from these documents is transforming Gitea (a lightweight Git platform) into a non-technical user-friendly office collaboration platform. Key ideas:

#### A. Gitea Functionality Mapping to Office Needs

| Office Need | Traditional Tool | Gitea Feature | User View |
|---|---|---|---|
| Project Space | Google Drive | Repository | "My Project" |
| Task Management | Trello | Issues + Projects | "Task Board" |
| Knowledge Base | Notion | Wiki | "Knowledge Center" |
| Document Collaboration | Google Docs | Markdown + PR | "Document Editor" |
| Approval Workflow | Approval Systems | Pull Request | "Approval Request" |
| File Storage | Dropbox | Repository Files + Git LFS | "File Management" |
| Team Discussion | Slack | Issue + Labels | "Team Chat" |
| Version Control | None | Git | "History & Versions" |
| Permissions | Scattered | Teams + Permissions | "Access Control" |

#### B. Architecture Design: "Everything is a Repository"

Every feature, plugin, workflow, and project is stored as an independent Git repository:
- Price monitoring plugin = repository with docker-compose, config, scripts
- Data analysis skill = repository with code, examples, tests
- Personal workspace = dedicated repository for daily memories in Markdown format
- Team project = repository with branches for different people's work

Key Advantages:
- Complete version control (who changed what, when, why)
- Easy one-click deployment via Docker
- Data completely isolated per user/project
- Full Git merge/diff/rollback capabilities
- Team collaboration without conflicts

#### C. Gitea + OpenClaw (AI Brain) Integration

OpenClaw's Role: Translate natural language to Gitea operations

User: "Help me create a competitor analysis project"
↓
OpenClaw (AI):
  1. Create repository: project-competitor-analysis
  2. Initialize folder structure
  3. Clone relevant plugins (price-monitor, news-aggregator, data-analyzer)
  4. Create Issues for setup tasks
  5. Notify team members
  
User sees: Clean interface with project ready to use
(No Git, branches, commits, or technical terms visible)

#### D. PR (Pull Request) + Branch System for Non-Technical Collaboration

Transform Git's powerful collaboration model into office scenarios:

Scenario 1: Document Review
- Employee creates "draft" version in personal workspace
- Submits for approval (= Pull Request)
- Manager reviews with inline comments, version comparison
- Once approved, changes merge to official version
- Complete audit trail: who approved, when, what changed

Scenario 2: Task Completion
- Task assigned to employee
- Employee completes work in personal branch
- Submits for verification (= PR)
- Manager reviews attached deliverables
- If approved, automatically marks task complete and archives result

Scenario 3: Personal Memory Archival
- Daily OpenClaw conversations auto-save to "draft" branch
- OpenClaw summarizes valuable items
- Creates PR to "official memory" branch
- User confirms → merges permanently into personal archive

#### E. Server Requirements

Excellent news: Gitea is extremely lightweight
- Minimum: 256MB RAM, can run on Raspberry Pi
- MVP: 2 cores, 4GB RAM, 50GB SSD = all you need for 10-20 person team
- 100-300MB base memory usage (vs GitLab's 4GB+)
- Private deployment possible (data under your control)

## 3. AI-DRIVEN TOOL DISCOVERY PLATFORM (Web Crawler Navigation)

A complete secondary product is documented in detail:

### Tool Navigation Website System

What: An AI tool discovery and comparison website that automatically collects, verifies, and displays information about software tools

Full Pipeline:
1. Discovery Layer: Automatically crawl 20-50 tool directory websites
2. Collection: Extract tool names, URLs, pricing, features from official pages
3. Cleaning: Deduplicate, normalize, resolve conflicts
4. Verification: Two-stage validation with evidence chains (source URL + timestamp + screenshot)
5. Database: Store with coverage scores and confidence ratings
6. Presentation: Web UI with filtering, comparison, sorting
7. Iteration: Continuous re-crawling every 3-30 days

MVP Requirements:
- 1000+ tools with 70%+ key field coverage
- Evidence chain for pricing/free tier/card requirement
- Table view with filtering, sorting, comparison
- All in 4 weeks of implementation

Tech Stack:
- crawler/src/collect.mjs — main scraper
- crawler/src/clean.mjs — deduplication
- Pinchtab (JavaScript rendering for dynamic sites)
- Crawlab (task scheduling)
- Scrapy (optional framework)

Three Execution Phases:
1. Phase A: Single site deep sampling (200 records per site)
2. Phase B: 3-site parallel collection with quality gates
3. Phase C: Full loop (180-min intervals, continuous)

## 4. AgentCrawl Platform Overview (Main Product)

Positioning: "AI-native office collaboration platform with Git-powered data sovereignty"

### Core Concept (Plan11 - Final Version)

A unified platform combining:
- Bottom: Gitea (Git version control, issue tracking, permissions)
- Middle: OpenClaw (AI task orchestration & code generation)
- Top: Custom web front-end (non-technical user interface)
- Deployment: Full private control (your own server)

### Key Differentiators

| Feature | AgentCrawl | Notion/Flybook | GitHub/GitLab |
|---|---|---|---|
| Data Control | 100% private | Vendor-locked | Vendor-locked |
| Technical Skill Required | Minimal | Minimal | High |
| Version History | Git (industrial) | Basic snapshots | Full Git |
| Resource Cost | $1,020/mo (20 people) | ~$5K/mo | $7K/mo |
| Customization | Unlimited | Constrained | Code-heavy |
| Price Model | SaaS $19-$240/mo/person | SaaS | SaaS/On-prem |

### Financial Projections (Year 1-3)

| Metric | Year 1 | Year 2 | Year 3 |
|---|---|---|---|
| Free Users | 1,000 | 4,000 | 10,000 |
| Paid Users | 75 | 300 | 750 |
| ARR | $45K | $180K | $450K |
| Total Revenue | $60K | $260K | $730K |
| Total Costs | $394K | $712K | $1,296K |
| Cumulative Profit | -$334K | -$786K | -$1,352K |
| Breakeven | — | — | Year 4 Q3 |

### Team Size Evolution

- Year 1: 3.5 people ($276K): Tech Lead, Backend, Frontend, DevOps (part-time)
- Year 2: 5.5 people ($432K): Add more Backend + Product Manager
- Year 3: 8.5 people ($780K): Add Frontend + Security Engineer

### Three Business Phases

Phase 1 (0-3 months): Core platform
- Gitea deployment + Adapter Gateway
- Web front-end (React + Vite)
- Lightweight mode (direct API calls)
- Validation: "new repo → new session → chat → generate README" works

Phase 2 (3-6 months): Advanced features
- Plugin system with security CI/CD
- Official data collection plugin
- High-level mode (OpenClaw integration)
- Validation: "Switch between modes, 30+ plugins available"

Phase 3 (6-12 months): Enterprise
- IM integration (Feishu, DingTalk, WeChat)
- Multi-user real-time collaboration
- Payment system (Stripe, WeChat Pay, Alipay)
- Validation: "3+ enterprise customers, SOC 2 certification"

### Plugin Architecture

Every feature is an optional plugin:
- Data collection plugin (Phase 2)
- Price monitoring plugin
- News aggregation plugin
- CRM integration plugin
- Financial approval plugin
- Custom plugins from community

Safety First: Complete CI/CD validation pipeline
- Docker image signature verification
- Dependency vulnerability scanning (Trivy + Snyk)
- Permission auditing (custom rule engine)
- README + test coverage checks
- Automatic PR rejection on failures

---

## 5. Key Technical Insights

### Why Gitea Over Alternatives?

vs. Spring若依 Framework:
- 若依 = bare skeleton, need to build everything from zero
- Gitea = complete product, just needs UI wrapper
- Gitea saves 6+ months of development for core features

vs. Notion/Flybook:
- Notion: Self-hosted? No. Customizable? No. Version control? Basic.
- Gitea: All three yes. Data is yours. Can modify everything.

vs. Open Source:
- OpenClaw supplier risk lowered (made optional in Phase 2)
- Gitea is MIT licensed, fully commercial-friendly
- No vendor lock-in

### Data Persistence Model

All information stored as Markdown in Git repositories:
- Conversations → Markdown files in personal repo
- Tasks → Gitea Issues (stored in Git)
- Documents → Wiki or README files
- Approvals → Pull Request history
- Everything: Permanent, versioned, auditable

OpenClaw's Daily Routine:
1. Collect all user conversations
2. Store in temporary "draft" branch
3. Summarize valuable content
4. Create PR to "official memory"
5. Auto-clean temporary files

- Complete planning, architecture, financial models, 18-month roadmap

2. Tool Navigation Website: AI-powered tool discovery crawler (Secondary)
- Complete data pipeline design
- MVP achievable in 4 weeks
- Currently being implemented

3. Fiction Writing Platform: (Tertiary/Future)
- Not extensively detailed
- Would leverage Gitea for chapter versioning
- Listed as Phase 3 expansion

All documents show sophisticated product thinking, market research, technical architecture, and financial modeling. The Gitea-based collaboration platform is the most thoroughly developed concept.
